METHOD     (TOF,PSD) 20- and 85-m flight paths. The data taken    1076800100024 
           at an 85-m flight path were normalized to those taken  1076800100025 
           at a 20-m flight path over the neutron energy from     1076800100026 
           300 eV to 1 keV. Pulse-shape discrimination was        1076800100027 
           employed to discriminate between fast neutrons and     1076800100028 
           gamma rays. The neutron flux from thermal-neutron      1076800100029 
           energies to 30 keV was measured with a parallel plate  1076800100030 
           10BF3 ionization chamber that intercepted the full     1076800100031 
           neutron stream.                                        1076800100032
